(**********************************************************************

 The enriched Kleisli category

 In this file we define an enrichment of the Kleisli category (that is
 not guaranteed to be univalent). There are a couple of interesting
 aspects to this construction.
 - The data is given in [Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment_data]. Most of
   the data corresponds directly to what one would expect from the
   Kleisli category. The hom object is given by the hom object from
   `E` but instantiated with the correct arguments, and the identity
   is given by the unit.
 - For composition in the enrichment, `postcomp_arr` is used. This
   significantly simplifies the usage of the obtained enrichment.
 - To prove the category laws in the enriched setting, one essentially
   follows the same proof strategy as for the ordinary case.

 In addition, we look at the universal property of the Kleisli category.
 We give a mapping property to construct functors from the Kleisli
 category ([functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment]), and we give a mapping
 property for natural transformations
 ([nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment]).

 Contents
 1. Data of the enrichment
 2. The laws of the enrichment
 3. The enrichment
 4. Enriched functors from the Kleisli category
 5. Natural transformations from the Kleisli category

 **********************************************************************)

  ⊗ (λ x0 y0 : Kleisli_cat_monad M, E ⦃ x0, M y0 ⦄) x

             · enriched_comp E x (M y) (M(M z))
             · postcomp_arr E x (μ M z)).

  (Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment_data ⦃ x, y ⦄) =

     (Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment_data ⦃ x, y ⦄)

    y

(g : Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ y, z ⟧),

       y z)

· (EM y (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x, M y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E x (M y) (M (M y))
   · postcomp_arr E x (μ M y))

· enriched_comp E (M x) (M (M y)) (M z)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M x) (M z) = ?b

· identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
  #⊗ ((EM x (M y) · postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y))
      #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y))
· postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M y) (M z) = ?b

        apply idpath.
      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
w, x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
  #⊗ ((EM x (M y) · postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y))
      #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y))
· postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M y) (M z) =
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· (postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
   · (EM (M y) (M z)
      · postcomp_arr E (M (M y)) (μ M z)))
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
  #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· (identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
   #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
   · enriched_comp E w (M (M y)) (M z))

   #⊗ ((EM x (M y) · postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y))
       #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
       · enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y))
   · (postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
      #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E w (M y) (M z))) =

   #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
   · (EM (M y) (M (M z))
      #⊗ identity
           ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
      · (postcomp_arr E (M (M y)) (μ M (M z) · μ M z)
         #⊗ identity
              ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
         · (identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
            #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
            · enriched_comp E w (M (M y)) (M z))))) =
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· (identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
   #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
   · (identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
      #⊗ (postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y)
          #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
      · (identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
         #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y)
         · (postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
            #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M y ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E w (M y) (M z)))))

V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
w, x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· (identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
   #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
   · (postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
      #⊗ identity
           ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
      · (mon_rassociator (E ⦃ M y, M z ⦄)
           (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
         · (mon_lassociator (E ⦃ M y, M z ⦄)
              (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
            · precomp_arr E (M z) (μ M y)
              #⊗ (identity (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄)
                  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
            · identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
              #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
            · enriched_comp E w (M (M y)) (M z))))) =
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· (identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
   #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
   · (EM (M y) (M (M z))
      #⊗ identity
           ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
      · (postcomp_arr E (M (M y)) (μ M (M z) · μ M z)
         #⊗ identity
              ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
         · (identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
            #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
            · enriched_comp E w (M (M y)) (M z)))))

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
w, x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
  #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ M y, M z ⦄)
    (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ M y, M z ⦄)
    (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· precomp_arr E (M z) (μ M y)
  #⊗ (identity (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄)
      #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
· enriched_comp E w (M (M y)) (M z) =
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
  #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· EM (M y) (M (M z))
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· postcomp_arr E (M (M y)) (μ M (M z) · μ M z)
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M (M y), M z ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
· enriched_comp E w (M (M y)) (M z)

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
w, x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
  #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· mon_rassociator (E ⦃ M y, M z ⦄)
    (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· mon_lassociator (E ⦃ M y, M z ⦄)
    (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· precomp_arr E (M z) (μ M y)
  #⊗ (identity (E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄)
      #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)) =
EM y (M z)
#⊗ identity ((E ⦃ x, M y ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· identity (E ⦃ M y, M (M z) ⦄)
  #⊗ (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· EM (M y) (M (M z))
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))
· postcomp_arr E (M (M y)) (μ M (M z) · μ M z)
  #⊗ identity ((E ⦃ M x, M (M y) ⦄) ⊗ (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄))

x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ y, z ⟧
enriched_to_arr E
  (mon_linvunitor (monoidal_unit V)
   · (enriched_from_arr E g #⊗ enriched_from_arr E f
      · (EM y (M z) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x, M y ⦄)
         · (postcomp_arr E (M y) (μ M z)
            #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x, M y ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E x (M y) (M z))))) = 
?b
V: monoidal_cat

E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ y, z ⟧
?b = f · bind g

      · (enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
         · postcomp_arr E w (μ M y)))) =
mon_linvunitor (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· (enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)
   #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y))

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E f #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
   · (enriched_comp E w (M x) (M (M y))
      · postcomp_arr E w (μ M y))) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E f #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· (EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
   · (postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y)
      #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y))) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E f #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w (M x) (M y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E f #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· EM x (M y) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)
· postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y)
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
(enriched_from_arr E f · EM x (M y)
 · postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y))
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)
#⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, M x ⦄)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M

f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E f · EM x (M y)
· postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E (# M f)
· postcomp_arr E (M x) (μ M y) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
x, y, w: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y) =
enriched_from_arr E (# M f · μ M y)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (** * 4. Enriched functors from the Kleisli category *)
  
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
is_functor_enrichment
  (λ x y : C, postcomp_arr E x (η M y))

  
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
is_functor_enrichment
  (λ x y : C, postcomp_arr E x (η M y))

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
∏ x : C,
enriched_id E x · postcomp_arr E x (η M x) =
enriched_id Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment
  (Left_Kleisli_functor M x)
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
∏ x y z : C,
enriched_comp E x y z · postcomp_arr E x (η M z) =
postcomp_arr E y (η M z) #⊗ postcomp_arr E x (η M y)
· enriched_comp Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment
    (Left_Kleisli_functor M x)
    (Left_Kleisli_functor M y)
    (Left_Kleisli_functor M z)
V: monoidal_cat

E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
enriched_from_arr Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment
  (# (Left_Kleisli_functor M) f) =
enriched_from_arr E f · postcomp_arr E x (η M y)

  Section FunctorFromKleisli.
    Context {C' : category}
            (E' : enrichment C' V)
            {F : C ⟶ C'}
            (EF : functor_enrichment F E E')
            {γ : M ∙ F ⟹ F}
            (Eγ : nat_trans_enrichment
                    γ
                    (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF)
                    EF)
            (p : ∏ (x : C), # F (η M x) · γ x = identity _)
            (q : ∏ (x : C), γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x).

    Definition functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data
      : functor_enrichment_data
          (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad M F γ p q)
          Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment
          E'
      := λ x y, EF x (M y) · postcomp_arr E' (F x) (γ y).

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF

# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
is_functor_enrichment
  functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data

# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
∏ x y z : Kleisli_cat_monad M,
enriched_comp Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment x y z
· functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data x z =
functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data y z
#⊗ functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data x y
· enriched_comp E'
    (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad M F γ p q x)
    (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad M F γ p q y)
    (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad M F γ p q z)

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF

identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
EM y (M z) #⊗ identity (E ⦃ x, M y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E x (M y) (M (M z))
· postcomp_arr E x (μ M z)
· functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data x z =
functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data y z
#⊗ functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data x y
· enriched_comp E' (F x) (F y) (F z)

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y, z: Kleisli_cat_monad M
(EM y (M z) · EF (M y) (M (M z))
 · postcomp_arr E' (F (M y)) (# F (μ M z) · γ z))
#⊗ EF x (M y) · enriched_comp E' (F x) (F (M y)) (F z) =
(EF y (M z) · postcomp_arr E' (F y) (γ z))
#⊗ (EF x (M y) · postcomp_arr E' (F x) (γ y))
· enriched_comp E' (F x) (F y) (F z)

γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E' (# F f · γ y) =
enriched_from_arr E f · EF x (M y)
· postcomp_arr E' (F x) (γ y)

        
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E' (# F f · γ y) =
enriched_from_arr E' (# F f)
· postcomp_arr E' (F x) (γ y)

        
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad M
f: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟦ x, y ⟧
enriched_from_arr E' (# F f · γ y) =
enriched_from_arr E' (# F f · γ y)

        apply idpath.
    Qed.

    Definition functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment
      : functor_enrichment
          (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad M F γ p q)
          Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment
          E'
      := functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data
         ,,
         functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_laws.

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
nat_trans_enrichment
  (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans M F γ p q)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment
     functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment) EF

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
nat_trans_enrichment
  (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans M F γ p q)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment
     functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment) EF

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
∏ x y : C,
EF x y
· precomp_arr E' (F y)
    (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans M F γ p
       q x) =
functor_comp_enrichment
  Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment
  functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment x y
· postcomp_arr E'
    ((Left_Kleisli_functor M
      ∙ functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad M F γ p q) x)
    (functor_from_kleisli_cat_monad_nat_trans M F γ p
       q y)

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: C
EF x y · precomp_arr E' (F y) (identity (F x)) =
postcomp_arr E x (η M y)
· functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data x y
· postcomp_arr E' (F x) (identity (F y))

postcomp_arr E x (η M y)
· functor_from_kleisli_cat_enrichment_data x y
· identity (E' ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF

· (EF x (M y) · postcomp_arr E' (F x) (γ y))

   · postcomp_arr E' (F x) (γ y))

q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: C
EF x y =
EF x y · postcomp_arr E' (F x) (# F (η M y) · γ y)

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V

E': enrichment C' V

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF

EF x y · identity (E' ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF

identity (F (functor_identity C x))

x, y: C
postcomp_arr E' (F x) (# F (η M y) · γ y) =
identity (E' ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M

E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'

  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: C
postcomp_arr E' (F x) (# F (η M y) · γ y) =
postcomp_arr E' (F x) (identity (F y))

      
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
F: C ⟶ C'
EF: functor_enrichment F E E'
γ: M ∙ F ⟹ F
Eγ: nat_trans_enrichment γ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EM EF) EF
p: ∏ x : C,
# F (η M x) · γ x =
identity (F (functor_identity C x))
q: ∏ x : C, γ (M x) · γ x = # F (μ M x) · γ x
x, y: C
# F (η M y) · γ y = identity (F y)

      apply p.
    Qed.
  End FunctorFromKleisli.

  (** * 5. Natural transformations from the Kleisli category *)
  
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
G₁, G₂: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟶ C'
EG₁: functor_enrichment G₁ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
EG₂: functor_enrichment G₂ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
α: Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₁
⟹ Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₂
Eα: nat_trans_enrichment α
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₁)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₂)
p: ∏ x : C,
# G₁ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x) · α x =
α (M x) · # G₂ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x)
nat_trans_enrichment
  (nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad M α p) EG₁ EG₂

  
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
G₁, G₂: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟶ C'
EG₁: functor_enrichment G₁ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
EG₂: functor_enrichment G₂ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
α: Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₁
⟹ Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₂
Eα: nat_trans_enrichment α
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₁)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₂)
p: ∏ x : C,
# G₁ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x) · α x =
α (M x) · # G₂ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x)
nat_trans_enrichment
  (nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad M α p) EG₁ EG₂

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
G₁, G₂: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟶ C'
EG₁: functor_enrichment G₁ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
EG₂: functor_enrichment G₂ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
α: Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₁
⟹ Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₂
Eα: nat_trans_enrichment α
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₁)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₂)
p: ∏ x : C,
# G₁ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x) · α x =
α (M x) · # G₂ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x)
∏ x y : Kleisli_cat_monad M,
EG₂ x y
· precomp_arr E' (G₂ y)
    (nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad M α p x) =
EG₁ x y
· postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x)
    (nat_trans_from_kleisli_cat_monad M α p y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
G₁, G₂: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟶ C'
EG₁: functor_enrichment G₁ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
EG₂: functor_enrichment G₂ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
α: Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₁
⟹ Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₂
Eα: nat_trans_enrichment α
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₁)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₂)
p: ∏ x : C,
# G₁ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x) · α x =
α (M x) · # G₂ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x)
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad M
EG₂ x y · precomp_arr E' (G₂ y) (α x) =
EG₁ x y · postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (α y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category
E': enrichment C' V
G₁, G₂: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟶ C'
EG₁: functor_enrichment G₁ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
EG₂: functor_enrichment G₂ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
α: Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₁
⟹ Left_Kleisli_functor M ∙ G₂
Eα: nat_trans_enrichment α
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₁)
  (functor_comp_enrichment
     Left_Kleisli_functor_enrichment EG₂)
p: ∏ x : C,
# G₁ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x) · α x =
α (M x) · # G₂ (kleisli_monad_nat_trans M x)
x, y: Kleisli_cat_monad M
q:= maponpaths
  (λ z : V ⟦ E ⦃ x, M y ⦄, E' ⦃ G₁ x, G₂ (M y) ⦄ ⟧,
   z
   · postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (# G₂ (identity (M y))))
  (nat_trans_enrichment_to_comp Eα x (M y)): postcomp_arr E x (η M (M y)) · EG₂ x (M y)
· precomp_arr E' (G₂ (M y)) (α x)
· postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (# G₂ (identity (M y))) =
postcomp_arr E x (η M (M y)) · EG₁ x (M y)
· postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (α (M y))
· postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (# G₂ (identity (M y)))
EG₂ x y · precomp_arr E' (G₂ y) (α x) =
EG₁ x y · postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (α y)

E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M

E': enrichment C' V

  (functor_comp_enrichment

· precomp_arr E' (G₂ (M y)) (α x)
· postcomp_arr E' (G₁ x) (# G₂ (identity (M y)))

  (functor_comp_enrichment

V: monoidal_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
M: Monad C
EM: monad_enrichment E M
C': category

G₁, G₂: Kleisli_cat_monad M ⟶ C'
EG₁: functor_enrichment G₁ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'
EG₂: functor_enrichment G₂ Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment E'

postcomp_arr E x (η M (M y))
· (postcomp_arr Kleisli_cat_monad_enrichment x
     (identity (M y)) · EG₁ x y) = EG₁ x y
